SHUGS KYI TSUL DU RGYAS BYUNG DANG CHA MNYAM DU RGYAS PA SOGS
SU 'GYUR RO ZHES SMRA'O, ,

DE LA KHO NA RE, RNAM SMIN GYI GZUGS CHOS CAN, KHYED LA RGYAS
BYUNG YOD PAR THAL, KHYOD RGYAS PA YOD PA GANG ZHIG ,DE RGYAS
PA YANG RGYAS BYUNG GI GZUGS LA LTOS PA'I PHYIR ZER NA MA
KHYAB, YANG, 'O NA, RNAM SMIN GYI RDUL RDZAS DANG, RGYAS BYUNG
GI RDUL RDZAS SO SO NAS GRUB PAR THAL,

'DOD NA, DBANG PO GZUGS CAN GCIG GI GO SA NA DBANG PO GZUGS
CAN RDZAS THA DAD PA GNYIS 'BYUNG BAR THAL LO, ,ZER NA SKYON
MED DE, MIG DBANG LTA BUR MTSON NA, DE'I TSOGS PA NA RNAM SMIN
DANG RGYAS BYUNG GI RDUL RDZAS RNAMS SO SO NAS YOD KYANG, DE
DAG CHA MNYAM 'DRES

PA'I TSUL DU GNAS PA LAS BSAGS PA'I GONG BU SO SOR MA GRUB PAS
RDUL RDZAS DE DAG GIS DON MIG DBANG GZUGS CAN PA GCIG BSKYED
PA LAS GNYIS BSKYED PA MA YIN NO, ,DE LA KHO NA RE, MIG DBANG
GCIG GI GO SA NA MIG DBANG RDZAS THA DAD PA GNYIS YOD PAR
THAL,

@010B DE'I GO SA NA RNAM SMIN GYI NGO BOR GYUR PA'I MIG DBANG
DANG, RGYAS BYUNG GI NGO BOR GYUR PA'I MIG DBANG GNYIS YOD PA
GANG ZHIG ,DE GNYIS RDZAS THA DAD CING PHAN TSUN GO SA 'GOG
NUS YIN PA'I PHYIR ZER NA MA KHYAB BYAS PA LA, DE GNYIS PHAN
TSUN GO SA 'GOG NUS MA YIN PAR THAL, DE GNYIS CHAR MIG

KHYAB CING, RNAM SMIN

DGE BA ZAG BCAS DANG MI DGE BA GANG RUNG GIS KHYAB PA'I PHYIR,
